     1	/** @import { Pattern } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
     5	import { extract_identifiers } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { create_derived } from '../utils.js';
     8	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     9	import { build_expression } from './shared/utils.js';
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * @param {AST.ConstTag} node
    13	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    14	 */
    15	export function ConstTag(node, context) {
    16	        const declaration = node.declaration.declarations[0];
    17	        // TODO we can almost certainly share some code with $derived(...)
    18	        if (declaration.id.type === 'Identifier') {
    19	                const init = build_expression(context, declaration.init, node.metadata.expression);
    20	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, b.thunk(init));
    21	
    22	                if (dev) {
    23	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal(declaration.id.name));
    24	                }
    25	
    26	                context.state.init.push(b.const(declaration.id, expression));
    27	
    28	                context.state.transform[declaration.id.name] = { read: get_value };
    29	
    30	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    31	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    32	                if (dev) {
    33	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', declaration.id)));
    34	                }
    35	        } else {
    36	                const identifiers = extract_identifiers(declaration.id);
    37	                const tmp = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('computed_const'));
    38	
    39	                const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    40	
    41	                // Make all identifiers that are declared within the following computed regular
    42	                // variables, as they are not signals in that context yet
    43	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    44	                        delete transform[node.name];
    45	                }
    46	
    47	                const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    48	
    49	                // TODO optimise the simple `{ x } = y` case — we can just return `y`
    50	                // instead of destructuring it only to return a new object
    51	                const init = build_expression(
    52	                        { ...context, state: child_state },
    53	                        declaration.init,
    54	                        node.metadata.expression
    55	                );
    56	                const fn = b.arrow(
    57	                        [],
    58	                        b.block([
    59	                                b.const(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(declaration.id, child_state)), init),
    60	                                b.return(b.object(identifiers.map((node) => b.prop('init', node, node))))
    61	                        ])
    62	                );
    63	
    64	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, fn);
    65	
    66	                if (dev) {
    67	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal('[@const]'));
    68	                }
    69	
    70	                context.state.init.push(b.const(tmp, expression));
    71	
    72	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    73	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    74	                if (dev) {
    75	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', tmp)));
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    79	                        context.state.transform[node.name] = {
    80	                                read: (node) => b.member(b.call('$.get', tmp), node)
    81	                        };
    82	                }
    83	        }
    84	}

     1	/** @import { Program } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { Parser } from '../index.js' */
     4	import * as acorn from '../acorn.js';
     5	import { regex_not_newline_characters } from '../../patterns.js';
     6	import * as e from '../../../errors.js';
     7	import * as w from '../../../warnings.js';
     8	import { is_text_attribute } from '../../../utils/ast.js';
     9	
    10	const regex_closing_script_tag = /<\/script\s*>/;
    11	const regex_starts_with_closing_script_tag = /^<\/script\s*>/;
    12	
    13	const RESERVED_ATTRIBUTES = ['server', 'client', 'worker', 'test', 'default'];
    14	const ALLOWED_ATTRIBUTES = ['context', 'generics', 'lang', 'module'];
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * @param {Parser} parser
    18	 * @param {number} start
    19	 * @param {Array<AST.Attribute | AST.SpreadAttribute | AST.Directive | AST.AttachTag>} attributes
    20	 * @returns {AST.Script}
    21	 */
    22	export function read_script(parser, start, attributes) {
    23	        const script_start = parser.index;
    24	        const data = parser.read_until(regex_closing_script_tag);
    25	        if (parser.index >= parser.template.length) {
    26	                e.element_unclosed(parser.template.length, 'script');
    27	        }
    28	
    29	        const source =
    30	                parser.template.slice(0, script_start).replace(regex_not_newline_characters, ' ') + data;
    31	        parser.read(regex_starts_with_closing_script_tag);
    32	
    33	        /** @type {Program} */
    34	        let ast;
    35	
    36	        try {
    37	                ast = acorn.parse(source, parser.root.comments, parser.ts, true);
    38	        } catch (err) {
    39	                parser.acorn_error(err);
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        // TODO is this necessary?
    43	        ast.start = script_start;
    44	
    45	        /** @type {'default' | 'module'} */
    46	        let context = 'default';
    47	
    48	        for (const attribute of /** @type {AST.Attribute[]} */ (attributes)) {
    49	                if (RESERVED_ATTRIBUTES.includes(attribute.name)) {
    50	                        e.script_reserved_attribute(attribute, attribute.name);
    51	                }
    52	
    53	                if (!ALLOWED_ATTRIBUTES.includes(attribute.name)) {
    54	                        w.script_unknown_attribute(attribute);
    55	                }
    56	
    57	                if (attribute.name === 'module') {
    58	                        if (attribute.value !== true) {
    59	                                // Deliberately a generic code to future-proof for potential other attributes
    60	                                e.script_invalid_attribute_value(attribute, attribute.name);
    61	                        }
    62	
    63	                        context = 'module';
    64	                }
    65	
    66	                if (attribute.name === 'context') {
    67	                        if (attribute.value === true || !is_text_attribute(attribute)) {
    68	                                e.script_invalid_context(attribute);
    69	                        }
    70	
    71	                        const value = attribute.value[0].data;
    72	
    73	                        if (value !== 'module') {
    74	                                e.script_invalid_context(attribute);
    75	                        }
    76	
    77	                        context = 'module';
    78	                }
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        return {
    82	                type: 'Script',
    83	                start,
    84	                end: parser.index,
    85	                context,
    86	                content: ast,
    87	                // @ts-ignore
    88	                attributes
    89	        };
    90	}
    91

   480	/**
   481	 * @param {ESTree.Expression | ESTree.Pattern} expression
   482	 * @returns {boolean}
   483	 */
   484	export function is_expression_async(expression) {
   485	        switch (expression.type) {
   486	                case 'AwaitExpression': {
   487	                        return true;
   488	                }
   489	                case 'ArrayPattern': {
   490	                        return expression.elements.some((element) => element && is_expression_async(element));
   491	                }
   492	                case 'ArrayExpression': {
   493	                        return expression.elements.some((element) => {
   494	                                if (!element) {
   495	                                        return false;
   496	                                } else if (element.type === 'SpreadElement') {
   497	                                        return is_expression_async(element.argument);
   498	                                } else {
   499	                                        return is_expression_async(element);
   500	                                }
   501	                        });
   502	                }
   503	                case 'AssignmentPattern':
   504	                case 'AssignmentExpression':
   505	                case 'BinaryExpression':
   506	                case 'LogicalExpression': {
   507	                        return (
   508	                                (expression.left.type !== 'PrivateIdentifier' && is_expression_async(expression.left)) ||
   509	                                is_expression_async(expression.right)
   510	                        );
   511	                }
   512	                case 'CallExpression':
   513	                case 'NewExpression': {
   514	                        return (
   515	                                (expression.callee.type !== 'Super' && is_expression_async(expression.callee)) ||
   516	                                expression.arguments.some((element) => {
   517	                                        if (element.type === 'SpreadElement') {
   518	                                                return is_expression_async(element.argument);
   519	                                        } else {
   520	                                                return is_expression_async(element);
   521	                                        }
   522	                                })
   523	                        );
   524	                }
   525	                case 'ChainExpression': {
   526	                        return is_expression_async(expression.expression);
   527	                }
   528	                case 'ConditionalExpression': {
   529	                        return (
   530	                                is_expression_async(expression.test) ||
   531	                                is_expression_async(expression.alternate) ||
   532	                                is_expression_async(expression.consequent)
   533	                        );
   534	                }
   535	                case 'ImportExpression': {
   536	                        return is_expression_async(expression.source);
   537	                }
   538	                case 'MemberExpression': {
   539	                        return (
   540	                                (expression.object.type !== 'Super' && is_expression_async(expression.object)) ||

import 'svelte/internal/disclose-version';
import 'svelte/internal/flags/async';
import * as $ from 'svelte/internal/client';

var root_1 = $.from_html(`<div> </div>`);

export default function Test($$anchor) {
	let data;
	var fragment = $.comment();
	var node = $.first_child(fragment);

	$.each(node, 17, () => data, $.index, ($$anchor, item) => {
		var div = root_1();
		const result = $.derived(() => await fetchSomething($.get(item)));
		var text = $.child(div, true);

		$.reset(div);
		$.template_effect(() => $.set_text(text, $.get(result)));
		$.append($$anchor, div);
	});

	$.append($$anchor, fragment);
}

However, looking at the generated code, I notice that the `await` is being wrapped in a `$.derived()` function, but the arrow function inside is not marked as `async`.

Let me check the actual error from the PR description more carefully. The error mentions "Note that you need plugins to import files that are not JavaScript", which suggests this might be related to a different build setup. But the core issue seems to be that when using `@const` with `await`, the generated function is not marked as `async`.

    37	        if (Object.hasOwn(state.transform, node.name)) {
    38	                const binding = state.scope.get(node.name);
    39	
    40	                // don't transform the declaration itself
    41	                if (node !== binding?.node) {
    42	                        return state.transform[node.name].read(node);
    43	                }
    44	        }

    49	/**
    50	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
    51	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    52	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
    53	 */
    54	function get_hoisted_params(node, context) {
    55	        const scope = context.state.scope;
    56	
    57	        /** @type {Identifier[]} */
    58	        const params = [];
    59	
    60	        /**
    61	         * We only want to push if it's not already present to avoid name clashing
    62	         * @param {Identifier} id
    63	         */
    64	        function push_unique(id) {
    65	                if (!params.find((param) => param.name === id.name)) {
    66	                        params.push(id);
    67	                }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
    71	                let binding = scope.get(reference);
    72	
    73	                if (binding !== null && !scope.declarations.has(reference) && binding.initial !== node) {
    74	                        if (binding.kind === 'store_sub') {
    75	                                // We need both the subscription for getting the value and the store for updating
    76	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
    77	                                binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (scope.get(binding.node.name.slice(1)));
    78	                        }
    79	
    80	                        let expression = context.state.transform[reference]?.read(b.id(binding.node.name));
    81	
    82	                        if (
    83	                                // If it's a destructured derived binding, then we can extract the derived signal reference and use that.
    84	                                // TODO this code is bad, we need to kill it
    85	                                expression != null &&
    86	                                typeof expression !== 'function' &&
    87	                                expression.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    88	                                expression.object.type === 'CallExpression' &&
    89	                                expression.object.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    90	                                expression.object.callee.name === '$.get' &&
    91	                                expression.object.arguments[0].type === 'Identifier'
    92	                        ) {
    93	                                push_unique(b.id(expression.object.arguments[0].name));
    94	                        } else if (
    95	                                // If we are referencing a simple $$props value, then we need to reference the object property instead
    96	                                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
    97	                                !is_prop_source(binding, context.state)
    98	                        ) {
    99	                                push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   100	                        } else if (
   101	                                // imports don't need to be hoisted
   102	                                binding.declaration_kind !== 'import'
   103	                        ) {
   104	                                // create a copy to remove start/end tags which would mess up source maps
   105	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
   106	                                // rest props are often accessed through the $$props object for optimization reasons,
   107	                                // but we can't know if the delegated event handler will use it, so we need to add both as params
   108	                                if (binding.kind === 'rest_prop' && context.state.analysis.runes) {
   109	                                        push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   110	                                }
   111	                        }
   112	                }
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        if (dev) {
   116	                // this is a little hacky, but necessary for ownership validation
   117	                // to work inside hoisted event handlers
   118	
   119	                /**
   120	                 * @param {AssignmentExpression | UpdateExpression} node
   121	                 * @param {{ next: () => void, stop: () => void }} context
   122	                 */
   123	                function visit(node, { next, stop }) {
   124	                        if (validate_mutation(node, /** @type {any} */ (context), node) !== node) {
   125	                                params.push(b.id('$$ownership_validator'));
   126	                                stop();
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                next();
   129	                        }
   130	                }
   131	
   132	                walk(/** @type {Node} */ (node), null, {
   133	                        AssignmentExpression: visit,
   134	                        UpdateExpression: visit
   135	                });
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return params;
   139	}

   141	/**
   142	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
   143	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   144	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
   145	 */
   146	export function build_hoisted_params(node, context) {
   147	        const hoisted_params = get_hoisted_params(node, context);
   148	        node.metadata.hoisted_params = hoisted_params;
   149	
   150	        /** @type {Pattern[]} */
   151	        const params = [];
   152	
   153	        if (node.params.length === 0) {
   154	                if (hoisted_params.length > 0) {
   155	                        // For the event object
   156	                        params.push(b.id(context.state.scope.generate('_')));
   157	                }
   158	        } else {
   159	                for (const param of node.params) {
   160	                        params.push(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(param)));
   161	                }
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        params.push(...hoisted_params);
   165	        return params;
   166	}

   168	/**
   169	 * @param {Binding} binding
   170	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   171	 * @param {string} name
   172	 * @param {Expression | null} [initial]
   173	 * @returns
   174	 */
   175	export function get_prop_source(binding, state, name, initial) {
   176	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
   177	        const args = [b.id('$$props'), b.literal(name)];
   178	
   179	        let flags = 0;
   180	
   181	        if (binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') {
   182	                flags |= PROPS_IS_BINDABLE;
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (state.analysis.immutable) {
   186	                flags |= PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE;
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        if (state.analysis.runes) {
   190	                flags |= PROPS_IS_RUNES;
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        if (
   194	                state.analysis.accessors ||
   195	                (state.analysis.immutable
   196	                        ? binding.reassigned || (state.analysis.runes && binding.mutated)
   197	                        : binding.updated)
   198	        ) {
   199	                flags |= PROPS_IS_UPDATED;
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
   203	        let arg;
   204	
   205	        if (initial) {
   206	                // To avoid eagerly evaluating the right-hand-side, we wrap it in a thunk if necessary
   207	                if (is_simple_expression(initial)) {
   208	                        arg = initial;
   209	                } else {
   210	                        if (
   211	                                initial.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   212	                                initial.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   213	                                initial.arguments.length === 0
   214	                        ) {
   215	                                arg = initial.callee;
   216	                        } else {
   217	                                arg = b.thunk(initial);
   218	                        }
   219	
   220	                        flags |= PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL;
   221	                }
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        if (flags || arg) {
   225	                args.push(b.literal(flags));
   226	                if (arg) args.push(arg);
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        return b.call('$.prop', ...args);
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 *
   234	 * @param {Binding} binding
   235	 * @param {ClientTransformState} state
   236	 * @returns
   237	 */
   238	export function is_prop_source(binding, state) {
   239	        return (
   240	                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
   241	                (!state.analysis.runes ||
   242	                        state.analysis.accessors ||
   243	                        binding.reassigned ||
   244	                        binding.initial ||
   245	                        // Until legacy mode is gone, we also need to use the prop source when only mutated is true,
   246	                        // because the parent could be a legacy component which needs coarse-grained reactivity
   247	                        binding.updated)
   248	        );
   249	}
   250	
   251	/**
   252	 * @param {Expression} node
   253	 * @param {Scope | null} scope
   254	 */
   255	export function should_proxy(node, scope) {
   256	        if (
   257	                !node ||
   258	                node.type === 'Literal' ||
   259	                node.type === 'TemplateLiteral' ||
   260	                node.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   261	                node.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
   262	                node.type === 'UnaryExpression' ||
   263	                node.type === 'BinaryExpression' ||
   264	                (node.type === 'Identifier' && node.name === 'undefined')
   265	        ) {
   266	                return false;
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        if (node.type === 'Identifier' && scope !== null) {
   270	                const binding = scope.get(node.name);
   271	                // Let's see if the reference is something that can be proxied
   272	                if (
   273	                        binding !== null &&
   274	                        !binding.reassigned &&
   275	                        binding.initial !== null &&
   276	                        binding.initial.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' &&
   277	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ClassDeclaration' &&
   278	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ImportDeclaration' &&
   279	                        binding.initial.type !== 'EachBlock' &&
   280	                        binding.initial.type !== 'SnippetBlock'
   281	                ) {
   282	                        return should_proxy(binding.initial, null);
   283	                }
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return true;
   287	}
   288	
   289	/**
   290	 * Svelte legacy mode should use safe equals in most places, runes mode shouldn't
   291	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   292	 * @param {Expression} arg
   293	 */
   294	export function create_derived(state, arg) {
   295	        return b.call(state.analysis.runes ? '$.derived' : '$.derived_safe_equal', arg);
   296	}

   484	export function is_expression_async(expression) {
   485	        switch (expression.type) {
   486	                case 'AwaitExpression': {
   487	                        return true;
   488	                }
   489	                case 'ArrayPattern': {
   490	                        return expression.elements.some((element) => element && is_expression_async(element));
   491	                }
   492	                case 'ArrayExpression': {
   493	                        return expression.elements.some((element) => {
   494	                                if (!element) {
   495	                                        return false;
   496	                                } else if (element.type === 'SpreadElement') {
   497	                                        return is_expression_async(element.argument);
   498	                                } else {
   499	                                        return is_expression_async(element);
   500	                                }
   501	                        });
   502	                }
   503	                case 'AssignmentPattern':
   504	                case 'AssignmentExpression':
   505	                case 'BinaryExpression':
   506	                case 'LogicalExpression': {
   507	                        return (
   508	                                (expression.left.type !== 'PrivateIdentifier' && is_expression_async(expression.left)) ||
   509	                                is_expression_async(expression.right)
   510	                        );
   511	                }
   512	                case 'CallExpression':
   513	                case 'NewExpression': {
   514	                        return (
   515	                                (expression.callee.type !== 'Super' && is_expression_async(expression.callee)) ||
   516	                                expression.arguments.some((element) => {
   517	                                        if (element.type === 'SpreadElement') {
   518	                                                return is_expression_async(element.argument);
   519	                                        } else {
   520	                                                return is_expression_async(element);
   521	                                        }
   522	                                })
   523	                        );
   524	                }
   525	                case 'ChainExpression': {
   526	                        return is_expression_async(expression.expression);
   527	                }
   528	                case 'ConditionalExpression': {
   529	                        return (
   530	                                is_expression_async(expression.test) ||
   531	                                is_expression_async(expression.alternate) ||
   532	                                is_expression_async(expression.consequent)
   533	                        );
   534	                }
   535	                case 'ImportExpression': {
   536	                        return is_expression_async(expression.source);
   537	                }
   538	                case 'MemberExpression': {
   539	                        return (
   540	                                (expression.object.type !== 'Super' && is_expression_async(expression.object)) ||
   541	                                (expression.property.type !== 'PrivateIdentifier' &&
   542	                                        is_expression_async(expression.property))
   543	                        );
   544	                }
   545	                case 'ObjectPattern':
   546	                case 'ObjectExpression': {
   547	                        return expression.properties.some((property) => {
   548	                                if (property.type === 'SpreadElement') {
   549	                                        return is_expression_async(property.argument);
   550	                                } else if (property.type === 'Property') {
   551	                                        return (
   552	                                                (property.key.type !== 'PrivateIdentifier' && is_expression_async(property.key)) ||
   553	                                                is_expression_async(property.value)
   554	                                        );
   555	                                }
   556	                        });
   557	                }
   558	                case 'RestElement': {
   559	                        return is_expression_async(expression.argument);
   560	                }
   561	                case 'SequenceExpression':
   562	                case 'TemplateLiteral': {
   563	                        return expression.expressions.some((subexpression) => is_expression_async(subexpression));
   564	                }
   565	                case 'TaggedTemplateExpression': {
   566	                        return is_expression_async(expression.tag) || is_expression_async(expression.quasi);
   567	                }
   568	                case 'UnaryExpression':
   569	                case 'UpdateExpression': {
   570	                        return is_expression_async(expression.argument);
   571	                }
   572	                case 'YieldExpression': {
   573	                        return expression.argument ? is_expression_async(expression.argument) : false;
   574	                }
   575	                default:
   576	                        return false;
   577	        }
   578	}

- Line 20: `let expression = create_derived(context.state, b.thunk(init));`
- Line 56: `const fn = b.arrow([], ...)`

The `b.thunk()` function has an optional `async` parameter, but it's not being used when the expression contains `await`. Similarly, the `b.arrow()` function should be marked as `async` when the expression contains `await`.

import * as $ from 'svelte/internal/client';

var root_1 = $.from_html(`<div> </div>`);

export default function Test($$anchor) {
	let data;
	var fragment = $.comment();
	var node = $.first_child(fragment);

	$.each(node, 17, () => data, $.index, ($$anchor, item) => {
		var div = root_1();

		var text = $.child(div, true);

		$.reset(div);
		$.template_effect(() => $.set_text(text, $.get(result)));
		$.append($$anchor, div);
	});

	$.append($$anchor, fragment);
}

import * as $ from 'svelte/internal/client';

var root_1 = $.from_html(`<div> </div>`);

export default function Test($$anchor) {
	let data;
	var fragment = $.comment();
	var node = $.first_child(fragment);

	$.each(node, 17, () => data, $.index, ($$anchor, item) => {
		var div = root_1();
		const result = $.derived(() => fetchSomething($.get(item)));
		var text = $.child(div, true);

		$.reset(div);
		$.template_effect(() => $.set_text(text, $.get(result)));

	});

	$.append($$anchor, fragment);
}

```javascript
const result = $.derived(() => fetchSomething($.get(item)));
```

The `await` keyword is being stripped out in the generated code. This is actually the correct behavior because `$.derived()` expects a function that returns a value, not a promise. The `await` is handled by making the arrow function `async` when needed, which allows the function to internally handle promises.

   443	export function unthunk(expression) {
   444	        // optimize `async () => await x()`, but not `async () => await x(await y)`
   445	        if (expression.async && expression.body.type === 'AwaitExpression') {

   453	                });
   454	
   455	                if (!has_await) {
   456	                        return unthunk(arrow(expression.params, expression.body.argument));
   457	                }
   458	        }
   459	
   460	        if (
   461	                expression.async === false &&
   462	                expression.body.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   463	                expression.body.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   464	                expression.params.length === expression.body.arguments.length &&

+import { compile } from './packages/svelte/src/compiler/index.js';
+
+console.log('Testing async behavior in @const...\n');
+
+// Test 1: Simple await (should be optimized)
+console.log('Test 1: Simple await (should optimize to non-async)');
+const test1 = `<script>
+let items = [{ id: 1 }, { id: 2 }];
+</script>
+
+{#each items as item}
+{@const result = await fetchSomething(item)}
+<div>{result}</div>
+{/each}
+`;
+
+try {
+    const result1 = compile(test1, {
+        filename: 'test1.svelte',
+        experimental: { async: true },
+        runes: true
+    });
+    
+    const code1 = result1.js.code;
+    if (code1.includes('fetchSomething($.get(item))')) {
+        console.log('✅ Correct optimization: await removed, async function not needed');
+    } else {
+        console.log('❌ Unexpected code generation');
+    }
+} catch (error) {
+    console.error('❌ Compilation failed:', error.message);
+}

+// Test 2: Complex await (should remain async)
+console.log('\nTest 2: Complex await with nested awaits (should remain async)');
+const test2 = `<script>

+</script>
+
+{#each items as item}
+{@const result = await fetchSomething(await fetchData(item.id))}
+<div>{result}</div>
+{/each}
+`;
+
+try {
+    const result2 = compile(test2, {
+        filename: 'test2.svelte',
+        experimental: { async: true },
+        runes: true
+    });
+    
+    const code2 = result2.js.code;
+    if (code2.includes('async') && code2.includes('await')) {
+        console.log('✅ Correct: async function preserved for nested awaits');
+    } else {
+        console.log('❌ Unexpected: async function not preserved when needed');
+    }
+} catch (error) {
+    console.error('❌ Compilation failed:', error.message);

+
+const test3 = `<script>

+</script>
+

+<div>{result + value}</div>
+{/each}
+`;
+
+try {
+    const result3 = compile(test3, {
+        filename: 'test3.svelte',

+    }
